  <w:LsdException Locked="false" Priority="72" SemiHidden="false"

</xml><![endif]--><!--[if gte mso 10]>
<![endif]--><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b><span style="line-height: 115%;">Spiritual Message for the Day – Sure Ways of Success in Life by Swami Krishnananda</span></b></span></p>
<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times Digest© | 20 May 2014 17:24 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><br style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;" /></span></span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr /><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
  <o:AllowPNG/>
 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
</xml><![endif]-->
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Sure Ways of Success in Life</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="text-align: center;" align="center"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Divine Life Society Publication: - </b><a href="http://www.swami-krishnananda.org/cult/cult_3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Resurgent Culture</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Swami Krishnananda</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">&nbsp;1.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Control the modifications of the mind-stuff in order to be able to have clear perception and true insight.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">2.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>We become normal only when we cease from thinking in terms of forms of the mental modification and begin to adopt quite a different way of perception. In other words, we have to rest in our own selves, first, in order that we may be healthy and also have a healthy perception of things.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">3.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>All types of objective thinking are considered in our system of Yoga as certain diseased conditions of consciousness, for in these states the consciousness is not-in-itself.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">4.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>A successful life, and a happy life, is possible only when one is able to adjust and adapt the different sides of the personality in a harmonious way and the entire personality with the others that form the constituents of the world. In this sense, life is an art.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">5.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The essence of art is the arrangement of material to produce rhythm, symmetry, order, fullness, and a sense of perfection so far as the mind can conceive of it. We have to arrange the pattern of life, with its forces of the outward Nature and inward impulses, so that there may not be any jarring element or inharmonious appearance unsuited to the purpose of realizing the equilibrium of the universe as reflected in our personal lives, in the life of society, the community, the nation and the world.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">6.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>A happy man who has been able to lead a successful life is one who is thoroughly friendly not only with the structural demands of his own body, mind, emotions, and intellect but also with the different elements that go to form the world outside.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">7.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Life is a preparation for self-accusation, a training ground for the individual to transfigure itself in a self-dedication to the Absolute Reality.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">8.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Our duty is to act, act in the right way, bearing in mind that we are fulfilling an inviolable and unavoidable imperative, not forced upon us by any outward mandate, but by the law of our own being.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">9.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The Bhagavad-Gita, exhorts us not to have attachment to things. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">10.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>To which object am I to be attached, when everything outside me is inseparably related to me, and we all mutually inclusive and determined in this magnificent home of God's creation?</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">11.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Every action has a reaction which comes with an equal force of nemesis and retribution, for every action is a sort of disturbance produced in the equilibrium of the universe, and the universe shall ever maintain its balance by rebutting the force of disturbance created in its being in the form of an action of thought.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">12.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The correct spirit with which we have to work in this world is one of self-sacrifice and surrender to the Supreme Cause of all things.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">13.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The correct perception is designated as Ishvaradrishti, the practice of the presence of God in each and everything, in every quarter and cranny, everywhere, and at all times.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">14.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The essence of the Gita teaching is this, that the universe is the body of God;&nbsp; it is God Himself appearing to us through our senses, the mind and the intellect, that there is nothing outside of God ever existent, that man is bound to have prosperity, victory, happiness and lawful polity when he acts with this consciousness—with the deep feeling that he is an instrument in the hands of the Absolute, that his actions are really not his but Its, and that suffering is inevitable the moment he cuts his consciousness off from the Divine. The happy and the normal life is, therefore, the Divine life.&nbsp;</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">15.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>To be successful in our different endeavors for perfection,&nbsp; first, we have to use our emotions properly and adjust them in such a way that they do not create any discord in life's harmonious process and secondly, we have always to attempt to make a fuller use of our personalities than we actually do in states of misconception, prejudice and ignorance.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">16.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Remember, always, that what is important is not so much what you are, as to what extent you know why you are what you are, and how much you Endeavour to improve yourselves in the right direction.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">17.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><em>Understand well</em> before you take a step. There cannot be a right attempt without a clear-cut ideal before it, and directing it. A race horse put to a plough or a plough horse put to race will not lead to any substantial result. We have to know our powers, our knowledge, and go only so far; not further.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">18.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The training of the emotions and the development of strength within, however, is not difficult for one who has a genuine conviction that he is backed up at all times by a mighty Power that works everywhere in the cosmos, and that he has nothing to fear. This faith should be born of conviction, enlightened understanding, and a real love for the Supreme Being.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">19.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Do not have inner conflicts. Such conflicts are mostly results of the inability to fulfil the basic instinctive urges, which, again, is due to ignorance of one's hidden capacities and of the way by which to utilize properly the facilities provided under the conditions in which one is placed. </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">20.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>You have to know clearly (1) what ought to be done, (2) what is capable of being done, (3) what has been done already, (4) why something has not been done yet, and (5) how to overcome the obstacles in a reasonable manner. This means that you have to be master of your own psychology.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">21.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>A successful life includes physical, emotional, intellectual and moral fitness based on an integration of being in all its degrees, inwardly as well as outwardly. Know yourselves as higher than you now are.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">22.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Summon the reserve forces which lie latent within, and use them for the constructive work of building the structure of life which is not merely yours, but of everyone, equally.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">23.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>When the diversity of beings is beheld as rooted in the One, and as having proceeded from the One, then does one attain to Perfection, says the Bhagavad-Gita. But the achievement of this end is hard, though possible for everyone. It demands inner toughness born of a perfect moral nature.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">24.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>A capacity to love and to serve all with the feeling of the presence of a common element behind everyone, to be truthful and honest and straightforward at any cost, to be able to feel for others as one does for oneself, not to do to others what would not be desirable for oneself, to have always a concern for the good of the whole world and not merely of a restricted group of persons, not to attempt at appropriating things which do not lawfully belong to one self, to be perfectly continent and restrained in thought, word and deed, to be able to look at the world with a cosmic vision, and to act at all times with this consciousness, is the requisite qualification demanded of a truly cultured person and a seeker of Truth.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">25.<span style="font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; -moz-font-feature-settings: normal; -moz-font-language-override: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Let us pray in the sublime words of the Upanishad: </span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;">Lead us from the unreal to the Real, </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"> Lead us from darkness to Light, </span><br /><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"> Lead us from death to Immortality.</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;" class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Excerpts from:</b></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: book antiqua,palatino;"><a href="http://www.swami-krishnananda.org/cult/cult_3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Sure Ways of Success in Life</b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Swami Krishnananda</b></span><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
